    2595             :     // Arrow 14 since https://github.com/apache/arrow/commit/95a8bfb319b2729c8f6daa069433caba3b4ddddd

    2601             : #if ARROW_VERSION_MAJOR >= 14
    2602             : #define GET_PTR_FROM_VALUES(var, type, values)                                 \
    2603             :     const auto var = static_cast<const type *>((values).get())
    2604             : #else
    2605             : #define GET_PTR_FROM_VALUES(var, type, values)                                 \
    2606             :     const auto var##tmp = std::static_pointer_cast<type>(values);              \
    2607             :     const auto var = var##tmp.get()
    2608             : #endif
